< Review>
Great stop if 299 is your route from Idaho or Eastern Oregon to Redding. Deli food, snacks and fully stocked grocery, including produce can meet any travelers' wants or needs. The staff is friendly & helpful and their bathroom is tidy & clean. Whole rotisserie chicken was delicious & only $6.99.  Just North of Mayers Hospital, it's super easy to find & fair priced fuel is right next door.</Review>

< Text>
Why people complain about this place I have no clue. It has good service, clean environment and good food for good price. I still feel this place is underrated. Enough with the 3 stars and below please!

This is our neighborhood spot for mexican food. Nuff said. We usually pig out after long hikes around Redwood Regional Park in Oakland or Tilden in Berkeley. After hiking over 8 miles you do get hungry for some burrito you know what I mean? ;)

Between the two of us we shared:
- spicy steak burrito
- 2 veg tamales as side dish

We always share the spicy steak burrito. It's a must try people!!! It's saucy and delicious. Not too light and not too heavy if you share it. Not enough for two people but too much for one so we usually split it and order a side dish like tamales and it works out great. The veg tamales were lovely. We ordered 1 red sauce and green to try. Both were unique and lovely.

Recently people had complained about change in service and ordering so was surprised to find out their service is still great as it used to be. No mess ups no confusion, no lateness. Friendly, fast and efficient.<//Text>

<text>This a nice restaurant, easily viewed from the street if you're driving by.  I had the taco salad with chicken.  It tasted fresh, meaty and the dressing had a very pleasant tang.  The chicken was very good quality, juicy and flavorful.  I also had the horchata and it was light and creamy with lots of cinnamon.  I noticed that they have beer choices in bottles and they have a children's menu.  I think I spied some high chairs as well. <UserId.>115694123052356676215<//UserId.><username>Alexander Ang-Angco</username><date>1450487056556</date><rate>2</rate>< text>
They are the sole Mexican restaurant in the neighborhood - so they have a monopoly on this flavor. Been coming here for years when there was a Korean(?) contingent running the kitchen and ordering. Since they've left wait times for food are awful, quality has dropped and this is hardly the best Mexican restaurant outside of Fruitvale - if you live in the area you would find La Catarina food truck on Broadway/29th. Go there coz that's where the Latino folk outside of Fruitvale go.< /text>
